        input.type = 'file';
        input.accept = '.json';
        input.onchange = function(e) {
            const file = e.target.files[0];
            if (file) {
                const reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = function(e) {
                    try {
                        const data = JSON.parse(e.target.result);
                        messages = data.messages || [];
                        selectedModelId = data.model || selectedModelId;
                        renderMessages();
                    } catch (error) {
                        alert('Geçersiz dosya formatı');
                    }
                };
                reader.readAsText(file);
            }
        };
        input.click();
    }

    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        setupFileUpload();
        setupKeyboardShortcuts();
        setupPWA();
        setupNotifications();
        setupOfflineMode();
        setupTypingIndicator();
        setupMessageTemplates();
        setupQuickReplies();
        setupScheduledMessages();
        setupMessageEncryption();
        setupContextMemory();
        setupRichTextEditor();
    });

    function setupContextMemory() {
        contextMemory = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('contextMemory') || '[]');
    }

    function addToContextMemory(message) {
        contextMemory.push({
            id: message.id,
            content: message.content,
            role: message.role,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            sentiment: analyzeSentiment(message.content)
        });

        if (contextMemory.length > 1000) {
            contextMemory = contextMemory.slice(-1000);
        }

        localStorage.setItem('contextMemory', JSON.stringify(contextMemory));
    }

    function speakText(text, voice = 'default') {
        if ('speechSynthesis' in window) {
            const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
            utterance.voice = speechSynthesis.getVoices().find(v => v.name.includes(voice)) || speechSynthesis.getVoices()[0];
            speechSynthesis.speak(utterance);
        }
    }

    function analyzeSentiment(text) {
        const positiveWords = ['güzel', 'harika', 'mükemmel', 'süper', 'wow'];
        const negativeWords = ['kötü', 'berbat', 'üzgün', 'kızgın', 'sinir'];

        const words = text.toLowerCase().split(' ');
        let score = 0;

        words.forEach(word => {
            if (positiveWords.includes(word)) score++;
            if (negativeWords.includes(word)) score--;
        });

        return score > 0 ? 'positive' : score < 0 ? 'negative' : 'neutral';
    }

    function setupRichTextEditor() {
        if (typeof Quill !== 'undefined' && document.getElementById('richTextEditor')) {
            richTextEditor = new Quill('#richTextEditor', {
                theme: 'snow',
                modules: {
                    toolbar: [
                        ['bold', 'italic', 'underline'],
                        ['blockquote', 'code-block'],
                        [{ 'header': 1 }, { 'header': 2 }],
                        [{ 'list': 'ordered'}, { 'list': 'bullet' }],
                        ['link', 'image'],
                        ['clean']
                    ]
                }
            });
        }
    }

    function setupPWA() {
        if (window.location.protocol === 'file:' || window.location.protocol === 'null:' ||
            window.location.hostname === 'localhost' || window.location.hostname === '127.0.0.1') {
            return;
        }

        if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
            navigator.serviceWorker.register('/sw.js').catch(console.error);
        }

        window.addEventListener('beforeinstallprompt', (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            deferredPrompt = e;
            showPWAInstallButton();
        });
    }

    function showPWAInstallButton() {
        const installBtn = document.createElement('button');
        installBtn.className = 'pwa-install';
        installBtn.textContent = 'Uygulamayı Yükle';
        installBtn.onclick = installPWA;
        document.body.appendChild(installBtn);
    }

    function installPWA() {
        if (deferredPrompt) {
            deferredPrompt.prompt();
            deferredPrompt.userChoice.then((choiceResult) => {
                deferredPrompt = null;
            });
        }
    }

    function setupNotifications() {
        if ('Notification' in window) {
            notificationPermission = Notification.permission;
            if (notificationPermission === 'default') {
                requestNotificationPermission();
            }
        }
    }

    function requestNotificationPermission() {
        Notification.requestPermission().then((permission) => {
            notificationPermission = permission;
        });
    }

    function setupOfflineMode() {
        window.addEventListener('online', () => {
            isOnline = true;
            hideOfflineIndicator();
        });

        window.addEventListener('offline', () => {
            isOnline = false;
            showOfflineIndicator();
        });
    }

    function showOfflineIndicator() {
        const indicator = document.createElement('div');
        indicator.className = 'offline-indicator';
        indicator.textContent = 'Çevrimdışı mod - Bağlantı kesildi';
        document.body.appendChild(indicator);
    }

    function hideOfflineIndicator() {
        const indicator = document.querySelector('.offline-indicator');
        if (indicator) indicator.remove();
    }

    function setupTypingIndicator() {
        const messageInput = document.getElementById('messageInput');
        if (messageInput) {
            messageInput.addEventListener('input', handleTyping);
        }
    }

    function handleTyping() {
        if (!isTyping) {
            isTyping = true;
        }

        clearTimeout(typingTimeout);
        typingTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
            isTyping = false;
        }, 1000);
    }

    function scrollToBottom() {
        const messagesArea = document.querySelector('.flex-1.overflow-y-auto.messages-panel');
        if (messagesArea) {
            messagesArea.scrollTop = messagesArea.scrollHeight;
        }
    }

    function setupMessageTemplates() {
        const templatesContainer = document.createElement('div');
        templatesContainer.id = 'messageTemplates';
        templatesContainer.className = 'hidden';
        templatesContainer.innerHTML = messageTemplates.map(template =>
            `<div class="message-template" onclick="useTemplate('${template}')">${template}</div>`
        ).join('');
        document.body.appendChild(templatesContainer);
    }

    function useTemplate(template) {
        document.getElementById('messageInput').value = template;
        document.getElementById('messageTemplates').classList.add('hidden');
    }

    function setupQuickReplies() {
        const quickRepliesContainer = document.createElement('div');
        quickRepliesContainer.id = 'quickReplies';
        quickRepliesContainer.className = 'hidden';
        quickRepliesContainer.innerHTML = quickReplies.map(reply =>
            `<button class="quick-reply" onclick="sendQuickReply('${reply}')">${reply}</button>`
        ).join('');
        document.body.appendChild(quickRepliesContainer);
    }

    function sendQuickReply(reply) {
        const message = {
            id: Date.now(),
            content: reply,
            role: 'user',
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        };
        messages.push(message);
        renderMessages();
        document.getElementById('quickReplies').classList.add('hidden');
    }

    function setupScheduledMessages() {
        setInterval(checkScheduledMessages, 60000);
    }

    function checkScheduledMessages() {
        const now = new Date();
        scheduledMessages.forEach((msg, index) => {
            if (new Date(msg.scheduleTime) <= now) {
                sendMessage({ preventDefault: () => {} });
                scheduledMessages.splice(index, 1);
            }
        });
    }

    function setupMessageEncryption() {
        if (typeof CryptoJS === 'undefined') {
            return;
        }
        encryptionKey = CryptoJS.lib.WordArray.random(256/8).toString();
    }

    function setupFileUpload() {
        const fileUploadArea = document.getElementById('fileUploadArea');
        const fileInput = document.getElementById('fileInput');

        fileUploadArea.addEventListener('click', () => fileInput.click());
        fileUploadArea.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            fileUploadArea.classList.add('dragover');
        });
        fileUploadArea.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
            fileUploadArea.classList.remove('dragover');
        });
        fileUploadArea.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            fileUploadArea.classList.remove('dragover');
            handleFileUpload(e.dataTransfer.files);
        });

        fileInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            handleFileUpload(e.target.files);
        });
    }

    function setupKeyboardShortcuts() {
        document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'k') {
                e.preventDefault();
                openSearchModal();
            }

            if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 's') {
                e.preventDefault();
                exportConversation();
            }

            if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'o') {
                e.preventDefault();
                importConversation();
            }

        });
    }

    // ============================================
    // RAG KÜTÜPHANESİ FONKSİYONLARI
    // ============================================
    let currentRAGMessageId = null;
    let ragCategories = [];
    let selectedCategoryColor = '#3b82f6';

    /**
     * Fallback RAG response formatter (Client-side processing hatası durumunda)
     */
    function formatRAGResponseFallback(rawData, query) {
        if (!rawData || !Array.isArray(rawData) || rawData.length === 0) {
            return "Üzgünüm, sorgunuzla ilgili bilgi bulunamadı.";
        }

        let response = `## RAG Kütüphanesi Sonuçları\n\n`;
        response += `Sorgunuzla ilgili kütüphanede **${rawData.length}** doküman bulundu.\n\n`;
        response += `---\n\n`;

        rawData.slice(0, 5).forEach((doc, index) => {
            response += `### ${index + 1}. ${doc.title || 'Başlıksız Doküman'}\n\n`;
            if (doc.relevance_score) {
                response += `**Benzerlik Skoru:** ${doc.relevance_score.toFixed(1)}%\n\n`;
            }
            if (doc.summary) {
                response += `**Özet:**\n${doc.summary}\n\n`;
            }
            if (doc.content) {
                const content = doc.content.length > 600 ? doc.content.substring(0, 600) + '...' : doc.content;
                response += `**İçerik:**\n${content}\n\n`;
            }
            response += `---\n\n`;
        });

        response += `*Bu bilgiler RAG kütüphanenizden alınmıştır.*`;
        return response;
    }

    // Modal'ı aç
    // RAG Kaynaklarını Göster/Gizle
    function toggleRAGSources(messageId) {
        const sourcesDiv = document.getElementById(`ragSources_${messageId}`);
        if (sourcesDiv) {
            sourcesDiv.classList.toggle('hidden');
            initializeIcons();
        }
    }

    // RAG Kaynak Seçimi
    function selectAllRAGSources(messageId) {
        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        if (!message || !message.ragSources) return;
        
        message.ragSources.forEach((source, idx) => {
            const checkbox = document.getElementById(`ragSource_${messageId}_${source.id || idx}`);
            if (checkbox) checkbox.checked = true;
        });
        updateRAGSourceSelection(messageId);
    }

    function updateRAGSourceSelection(messageId) {
        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        if (!message || !message.ragSources) return;
        
        let selectedCount = 0;
        message.ragSources.forEach((source, idx) => {
            const checkbox = document.getElementById(`ragSource_${messageId}_${source.id || idx}`);
            if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) selectedCount++;
        });
        
        const countSpan = document.getElementById(`ragSelectedCount_${messageId}`);
        if (countSpan) countSpan.textContent = selectedCount;
    }

    function reuseRAGSources(messageId) {
        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        if (!message || !message.ragSources) return;
        
        const selectedSources = [];
        message.ragSources.forEach((source, idx) => {
            const checkbox = document.getElementById(`ragSource_${messageId}_${source.id || idx}`);
            if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
                selectedSources.push(source.id);
            }
        });
        
        if (selectedSources.length === 0) {
            alert('Lütfen en az bir kaynak seçin');
            return;
        }
        
        // Seçilen kaynakları kullanarak yeni bir mesaj gönder
        const userMessage = prompt('Yeni sorunuzu girin:');
        if (!userMessage) return;
        
        // Seçilen kaynakları kullanarak mesaj gönder
        sendMessageWithSelectedRAGSources(userMessage, selectedSources);
    }

    function sendMessageWithSelectedRAGSources(userMessage, selectedSourceIds) {
        // Bu fonksiyon seçilen RAG kaynaklarını kullanarak yeni bir mesaj gönderir
        // Şimdilik normal mesaj gönderme fonksiyonunu kullanıyoruz
        // İleride backend'de seçili kaynakları kullanacak şekilde geliştirilebilir
        const input = document.getElementById('messageInput');
        if (input) {
            input.value = userMessage;
            sendMessageNormal();
        }
    }

    // RAG Kaynak Karşılaştırma
    function compareRAGSources(messageId) {
        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        if (!message || !message.ragSources) return;
        
        const selectedSources = [];
        message.ragSources.forEach((source, idx) => {
            const checkbox = document.getElementById(`ragSource_${messageId}_${source.id || idx}`);
            if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
                selectedSources.push(source);
            }
        });
        
        if (selectedSources.length < 2) {
            alert('Karşılaştırma için en az 2 kaynak seçmelisiniz');
            return;
        }
        
        if (selectedSources.length > 5) {
            alert('Maksimum 5 kaynak karşılaştırılabilir');
            return;
        }
        
        // Karşılaştırma modalını aç
        openRAGComparisonModal(messageId, selectedSources);
    }

    function openRAGComparisonModal(messageId, sources) {
        // Karşılaştırma modalını oluştur ve göster
        const cols = Math.min(sources.length, 3);
        let modalHTML = `
        <div id="ragComparisonModal" class="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 z-[10000] flex items-center justify-center p-4">
            <div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl max-w-6xl w-full max-h-[90vh] overflow-hidden flex flex-col">
                <div class="px-6 py-4 border-b border-slate-200 flex items-center justify-between">
                    <h3 class="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2">
                        <i data-lucide="git-compare" class="w-5 h-5 text-blue-600"></i>
                        RAG Kaynak Karşılaştırması (${sources.length} kaynak)
                    </h3>
                    <button onclick="closeRAGComparisonModal()" class="p-1.5 hover:bg-slate-100 rounded-full transition-colors">
                        <i data-lucide="x" class="w-5 h-5 text-slate-500"></i>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <div class="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6">
                    <div class="grid grid-cols-${cols} gap-4">
        `;
        
        sources.forEach((source, idx) => {
            modalHTML += `
                <div class="bg-slate-50 rounded-lg p-4 border border-slate-200">
                    <div class="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                        <h4 class="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-800">Kaynak ${idx + 1}</h4>
                        ${source.relevance_score ? `
                        <span class="text-xs px-2 py-1 bg-emerald-100 text-emerald-700 rounded-full">
                            %${source.relevance_score.toFixed(1)}
                        </span>
                        ` : ''}
                    </div>
                    <h5 class="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-700 mb-2">${escapeHtml(source.title || 'Başlıksız')}</h5>
                    ${source.summary ? `
                    <p class="text-xs text-slate-600 mb-2 line-clamp-4">${escapeHtml(source.summary)}</p>
                    ` : ''}
                    ${source.tags && Array.isArray(source.tags) && source.tags.length > 0 ? `
                    <div class="flex flex-wrap gap-1 mt-2">
                        ${source.tags.map(tag => `
                        <span class="text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-slate-200 text-slate-700 rounded">${escapeHtml(tag)}</span>
                        `).join('')}
                    </div>
                    ` : ''}
                </div>
            `;
        });
        
        modalHTML += `
                    </div>
                    <div class="mt-6 p-4 bg-blue-50 rounded-lg border border-blue-200">
                        <h4 class="text-sm font-semibold text-blue-800 mb-2 flex items-center gap-2">
                            <i data-lucide="info" class="w-4 h-4"></i>
                            Karşılaştırma Özeti
                        </h4>
                        <div class="text-xs text-blue-700 space-y-1">
                            <p>• <strong>Ortak Etiketler:</strong> ${getCommonTags(sources).join(', ') || 'Yok'}</p>
                            <p>• <strong>Ortalama Benzerlik:</strong> %${getAverageScore(sources).toFixed(1)}</p>
                            <p>• <strong>En Yüksek Skor:</strong> %${getMaxScore(sources).toFixed(1)}</p>
                            <p>• <strong>En Düşük Skor:</strong> %${getMinScore(sources).toFixed(1)}</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="px-6 py-4 border-t border-slate-200 flex justify-end">
                    <button onclick="closeRAGComparisonModal()" class="px-4 py-2 text-sm bg-slate-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-slate-700 transition-colors">
                        Kapat
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        `;
        
        // Modal'ı ekle
        const existingModal = document.getElementById('ragComparisonModal');
        if (existingModal) {
            existingModal.remove();
        }
        
        document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', modalHTML);
        initializeIcons();
    }

    function closeRAGComparisonModal() {
        const modal = document.getElementById('ragComparisonModal');
        if (modal) {
            modal.remove();
        }
    }

    function getCommonTags(sources) {
        if (!sources || sources.length === 0) return [];
        const allTags = sources.map(s => s.tags || []).filter(t => Array.isArray(t) && t.length > 0);
        if (allTags.length === 0) return [];
        
        const firstTags = allTags[0];
        return firstTags.filter(tag => allTags.every(tags => tags.includes(tag)));
    }

    function getAverageScore(sources) {
        const scores = sources.map(s => s.relevance_score || 0).filter(s => s > 0);
        if (scores.length === 0) return 0;
        return scores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / scores.length;
    }

    function getMaxScore(sources) {
        const scores = sources.map(s => s.relevance_score || 0);
        return Math.max(...scores, 0);
    }

    function getMinScore(sources) {
        const scores = sources.map(s => s.relevance_score || 0).filter(s => s > 0);
        if (scores.length === 0) return 0;
        return Math.min(...scores);
    }

    // RAG Sonuç Güncelleme
    async function refreshRAGSources(messageId) {
        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        if (!message) return;
        
        // Kullanıcı mesajını bul
        const messageIndex = messages.findIndex(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        if (messageIndex === 0) {
            alert('Kullanıcı mesajı bulunamadı');
            return;
        }
        
        const userMessage = messages[messageIndex - 1];
        if (!userMessage || userMessage.role !== 'user') {
            alert('Kullanıcı mesajı bulunamadı');
            return;
        }
        
        // Yenileme butonunu devre dışı bırak
        const refreshBtn = event.target.closest('button');
        if (refreshBtn) {
            refreshBtn.disabled = true;
            refreshBtn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="loader-2" class="w-4 h-4 animate-spin"></i>';
            initializeIcons();
        }
        
        try {
            // Backend'den yeni RAG sonuçlarını al
            const formData = new FormData();
            formData.append('message', userMessage.content);
            formData.append('rag_mode', message.ragMode || 'rag_ai');
            
            // Mevcut filtreleri gönder
            if (message.ragFilters) {
                if (message.ragFilters.minScore) formData.append('rag_min_score', message.ragFilters.minScore);
                if (message.ragFilters.categoryId) formData.append('rag_category_id', message.ragFilters.categoryId);
                if (message.ragFilters.sortBy) formData.append('rag_sort_by', message.ragFilters.sortBy);
                if (message.ragFilters.dateFrom) formData.append('rag_date_from', message.ragFilters.dateFrom);
                if (message.ragFilters.dateTo) formData.append('rag_date_to', message.ragFilters.dateTo);
            }
            
            const response = await fetch('https://www.hepbilen.com/Multipurposectr/get_rag_context_refresh', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            });
            
            const data = await response.json();
            
            if (data.success && data.rag_sources) {
                // Mesajın RAG kaynaklarını güncelle
                message.ragSources = data.rag_sources;
                
                // Mesajı yeniden render et
                renderMessages();
                
                // Başarı mesajı göster
                showNotification('RAG sonuçları başarıyla güncellendi', 'success');
            } else {
                throw new Error(data.message || 'Güncelleme başarısız');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('RAG güncelleme hatası:', error);
            showNotification('RAG sonuçları güncellenirken bir hata oluştu', 'error');
        } finally {
            // Yenileme butonunu tekrar etkinleştir
            if (refreshBtn) {
                refreshBtn.disabled = false;
                refreshBtn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="refresh-cw" class="w-4 h-4"></i>';
                initializeIcons();
            }
        }
    }

    function showNotification(message, type = 'info') {
        // Basit bildirim gösterimi
        const notification = document.createElement('div');
        notification.className = `fixed top-4 right-4 px-4 py-3 rounded-lg shadow-lg z-[10001] ${
            type === 'success' ? 'bg-emerald-500 text-white' :
            type === 'error' ? 'bg-red-500 text-white' :
            'bg-blue-500 text-white'
        }`;
        notification.textContent = message;
        document.body.appendChild(notification);
        
        setTimeout(() => {
            notification.remove();
        }, 3000);
    }

                                    <div class="font-medium text-slate-800">PDF Export</div>

    function closeRAGShareModal() {
        const modal = document.getElementById('ragShareModal');
        if (modal) {

        }
    }

    async function exportRAGSources(format, messageId) {
        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        if (!message || !message.ragSources) return;
        
        try {
            if (format === 'link') {
                // Link oluştur
                const shareData = {
                    messageId: messageId,
                    sources: message.ragSources,
                    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                };
                
                // Base64 encode
                const encoded = btoa(JSON.stringify(shareData));
                const shareLink = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname + '?rag_share=' + encoded;
                
                // Kopyala
                await navigator.clipboard.writeText(shareLink);
                showNotification('Link panoya kopyalandı!', 'success');
                closeRAGShareModal();
            } else if (format === 'json') {
                // JSON export
                const jsonData = {
                    messageId: messageId,
                    sources: message.ragSources,
                    exportedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
                    version: '1.0'
                };
                
                const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(jsonData, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
                const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
                const a = document.createElement('a');
                a.href = url;
                a.download = `rag_sources_${messageId}_${Date.now()}.json`;
                a.click();
                URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
                
                showNotification('JSON dosyası indirildi!', 'success');
                closeRAGShareModal();
            } else if (format === 'pdf') {
                // PDF export (basit HTML to PDF)
                const pdfContent = generateRAGPDFContent(message.ragSources);
                const printWindow = window.open('', '_blank');
                printWindow.document.write(pdfContent);
                printWindow.document.close();
                printWindow.print();
                
                showNotification('PDF oluşturuldu!', 'success');
                closeRAGShareModal();
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Export hatası:', error);
            showNotification('Export sırasında bir hata oluştu', 'error');
        }
    }

    function generateRAGPDFContent(sources) {
        let html = `
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
        <head>
            <title>RAG Kaynakları</title>
            <style>
                body { font-family: Arial, sans-serif; padding: 20px; }
                h1 { color: #059669; }
                .source { margin-bottom: 20px; padding: 15px; border: 1px solid #ddd; border-radius: 8px; }
                .source-title { font-weight: bold; font-size: 16px; margin-bottom: 10px; }
                .source-score { color: #059669; font-weight: bold; }
                .source-summary { margin-top: 10px; color: #666; }
            </style>
        </head>
        <body>
            <h1>RAG Kütüphanesi Kaynakları</h1>
            <p>Oluşturulma Tarihi: ${new Date().toLocaleString('tr-TR')}</p>
            <hr>
        `;
        
        sources.forEach((source, idx) => {
            html += `
            <div class="source">
                <div class="source-title">Kaynak ${idx + 1}: ${escapeHtml(source.title || 'Başlıksız')}</div>
                ${source.relevance_score ? `<div class="source-score">Benzerlik Skoru: %${source.relevance_score.toFixed(1)}</div>` : ''}
                ${source.summary ? `<div class="source-summary">${escapeHtml(source.summary)}</div>` : ''}
                ${source.tags && Array.isArray(source.tags) && source.tags.length > 0 ? `
                <div style="margin-top: 10px;">
                    <strong>Etiketler:</strong> ${source.tags.map(t => escapeHtml(t)).join(', ')}
                </div>
                ` : ''}
            </div>
            `;
        });
        
        html += `
        </body>
        </html>
        `;
        
        return html;
    }

    // RAG Sonuç Yorumlama
    function addRAGAnnotation(messageId, sourceId) {
        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        if (!message || !message.ragSources) return;
        
        const source = message.ragSources.find(s => (s.id || message.ragSources.indexOf(s)) === sourceId);
        if (!source) return;
        
        const existingNote = source.annotation || '';
        const note = prompt('Bu kaynak için bir not ekleyin:', existingNote);
        
        if (note !== null) {
            if (!source.annotation) {
                source.annotation = '';
            }
            source.annotation = note;
            
            // Backend'e kaydet
            saveRAGAnnotation(messageId, sourceId, note);
            
            // Mesajı yeniden render et
            renderMessages();
            
            if (note) {
                showNotification('Not başarıyla kaydedildi', 'success');
            } else {
                showNotification('Not silindi', 'info');
            }
        }
    }

    function viewRAGAnnotation(messageId, sourceId) {
        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        if (!message || !message.ragSources) return;
        
        const source = message.ragSources.find(s => (s.id || message.ragSources.indexOf(s)) === sourceId);
        if (!source || !source.annotation) return;
        
        alert('Not:\n\n' + source.annotation);
    }

    function toggleRAGFavorite(messageId, sourceId) {
        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        if (!message || !message.ragSources) return;
        
        const source = message.ragSources.find(s => (s.id || message.ragSources.indexOf(s)) === sourceId);
        if (!source) return;
        
        source.isFavorite = !source.isFavorite;
        
        // Backend'e kaydet
        saveRAGFavorite(messageId, sourceId, source.isFavorite);
        
        // Mesajı yeniden render et
        renderMessages();
        
        showNotification(source.isFavorite ? 'Favorilere eklendi' : 'Favorilerden çıkarıldı', 'success');
    }

    async function saveRAGAnnotation(messageId, sourceId, annotation) {
        try {
            const formData = new FormData();
            formData.append('message_id', messageId);
            formData.append('source_id', sourceId);
            formData.append('annotation', annotation);
            
            await fetch('https://www.hepbilen.com/Multipurposectr/save_rag_annotation', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            });
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Not kaydetme hatası:', error);
        }
    }

    async function saveRAGFavorite(messageId, sourceId, isFavorite) {
        try {
            const formData = new FormData();
            formData.append('message_id', messageId);
            formData.append('source_id', sourceId);
            formData.append('is_favorite', isFavorite ? '1' : '0');
            
            await fetch('https://www.hepbilen.com/Multipurposectr/save_rag_favorite', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            });
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Favori kaydetme hatası:', error);
        }
    }

    // RAG Sonuç Analizi
    function showRAGAnalytics(messageId) {
        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        if (!message || !message.ragSources) return;
        
        const sources = message.ragSources;
        
        // İstatistikleri hesapla
        const stats = calculateRAGStats(sources);
        
        // Analiz modalını aç
        openRAGAnalyticsModal(messageId, sources, stats);
    }

    function calculateRAGStats(sources) {
        const scores = sources.map(s => s.relevance_score || 0).filter(s => s > 0);
        const tags = sources.flatMap(s => s.tags || []).filter(t => t);
        const categories = sources.map(s => s.category_id).filter(c => c);
        
        // Tag sayıları
        const tagCounts = {};
        tags.forEach(tag => {
            tagCounts[tag] = (tagCounts[tag] || 0) + 1;
        });
        
        // Kategori sayıları
        const categoryCounts = {};
        categories.forEach(cat => {
            categoryCounts[cat] = (categoryCounts[cat] || 0) + 1;
        });
        
        return {
            totalSources: sources.length,
            averageScore: scores.length > 0 ? scores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / scores.length : 0,
            maxScore: scores.length > 0 ? Math.max(...scores) : 0,
            minScore: scores.length > 0 ? Math.min(...scores) : 0,
            scoreDistribution: {
                high: scores.filter(s => s >= 70).length,
                medium: scores.filter(s => s >= 40 && s < 70).length,
                low: scores.filter(s => s < 40).length
            },
            topTags: Object.entries(tagCounts)
                .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
                .slice(0, 5)
                .map(([tag, count]) => ({ tag, count })),
            categoryDistribution: Object.entries(categoryCounts)
                .map(([cat, count]) => ({ category: cat, count }))
        };
    }

    function openRAGAnalyticsModal(messageId, sources, stats) {
        let modalHTML = `
        <div id="ragAnalyticsModal" class="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 z-[10000] flex items-center justify-center p-4">
            <div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl max-w-4xl w-full max-h-[90vh] overflow-hidden flex flex-col">
                <div class="px-6 py-4 border-b border-slate-200 flex items-center justify-between">
                    <h3 class="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2">
                        <i data-lucide="bar-chart-3" class="w-5 h-5 text-purple-600"></i>
                        RAG Sonuç Analizi
                    </h3>
                    <button onclick="closeRAGAnalyticsModal()" class="p-1.5 hover:bg-slate-100 rounded-full transition-colors">
                        <i data-lucide="x" class="w-5 h-5 text-slate-500"></i>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <div class="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-6">
                    <!-- Genel İstatistikler -->
                    <div class="grid grid-cols-4 gap-4">
                        <div class="bg-emerald-50 rounded-lg p-4 border border-emerald-200">
                            <div class="text-xs text-emerald-600 font-medium mb-1">Toplam Kaynak</div>
                            <div class="text-2xl font-bold text-emerald-700">${stats.totalSources}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="bg-blue-50 rounded-lg p-4 border border-blue-200">
                            <div class="text-xs text-blue-600 font-medium mb-1">Ortalama Skor</div>
                            <div class="text-2xl font-bold text-blue-700">%${stats.averageScore.toFixed(1)}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="bg-purple-50 rounded-lg p-4 border border-purple-200">
                            <div class="text-xs text-purple-600 font-medium mb-1">En Yüksek</div>
                            <div class="text-2xl font-bold text-purple-700">%${stats.maxScore.toFixed(1)}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="bg-amber-50 rounded-lg p-4 border border-amber-200">
                            <div class="text-xs text-amber-600 font-medium mb-1">En Düşük</div>
                            <div class="text-2xl font-bold text-amber-700">%${stats.minScore.toFixed(1)}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <!-- Skor Dağılımı -->
                    <div class="bg-slate-50 rounded-lg p-4 border border-slate-200">
                        <h4 class="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-800 mb-3">Benzerlik Skoru Dağılımı</h4>
                        <div class="space-y-2">
                            <div class="flex items-center justify-between">
                                <span class="text-xs text-slate-600">Yüksek (≥70%)</span>
                                <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                                    <div class="w-32 h-2 bg-slate-200 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                                        <div class="h-full bg-emerald-500 rounded-full" style="width: ${(stats.scoreDistribution.high / stats.totalSources) * 100}%"></div>
                                    </div>
                                    <span class="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-700 w-8 text-right">${stats.scoreDistribution.high}</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="flex items-center justify-between">
                                <span class="text-xs text-slate-600">Orta (40-70%)</span>
                                <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                                    <div class="w-32 h-2 bg-slate-200 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                                        <div class="h-full bg-blue-500 rounded-full" style="width: ${(stats.scoreDistribution.medium / stats.totalSources) * 100}%"></div>
                                    </div>
                                    <span class="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-700 w-8 text-right">${stats.scoreDistribution.medium}</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="flex items-center justify-between">
                                <span class="text-xs text-slate-600">Düşük (<40%)</span>
                                <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                                    <div class="w-32 h-2 bg-slate-200 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                                        <div class="h-full bg-amber-500 rounded-full" style="width: ${(stats.scoreDistribution.low / stats.totalSources) * 100}%"></div>
                                    </div>
                                    <span class="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-700 w-8 text-right">${stats.scoreDistribution.low}</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <!-- En Çok Kullanılan Etiketler -->
                    ${stats.topTags.length > 0 ? `
                    <div class="bg-slate-50 rounded-lg p-4 border border-slate-200">
                        <h4 class="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-800 mb-3">En Çok Kullanılan Etiketler</h4>
                        <div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                            ${stats.topTags.map(t => `
                            <span class="px-3 py-1.5 bg-white border border-slate-300 rounded-lg text-xs font-medium text-slate-700">
                                ${escapeHtml(t.tag)} <span class="text-slate-500">(${t.count})</span>
                            </span>
                            `).join('')}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    ` : ''}
                </div>
                <div class="px-6 py-4 border-t border-slate-200 flex justify-end">
                    <button onclick="closeRAGAnalyticsModal()" class="px-4 py-2 text-sm bg-slate-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-slate-700 transition-colors">
                        Kapat
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        `;
        
        const existingModal = document.getElementById('ragAnalyticsModal');
        if (existingModal) {
            existingModal.remove();
        }
        
        document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', modalHTML);
        initializeIcons();
    }

    function closeRAGAnalyticsModal() {
        const modal = document.getElementById('ragAnalyticsModal');
        if (modal) {
            modal.remove();
        }
    }

    async function openRAGLibraryModal(messageId) {
        // UyeSeviye kontrolü - Seviye < 2 ise uyarı göster
        if (typeof window.USER_LEVEL !== 'undefined' && window.USER_LEVEL < 2) {
            alert('RAG kütüphanesi özelliği sadece Premium üyeler için kullanılabilir. Lütfen Premium üyeliğe yükseltin.');
            return;
        }
        
        currentRAGMessageId = messageId;
        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === messageId);
        
        if (!message) {
            alert('Mesaj bulunamadı');
            return;
        }

        // İçerik önizlemesini hazırla
        let content = '';
        if (message.role === 'assistant') {
            // Assistant mesajı - tüm sohbeti veya sadece bu mesajı
            const messageIndex = messages.findIndex(msg => msg.id === messageId);
            if (messageIndex > 0) {
                // Önceki kullanıcı mesajını da ekle
                const userMessage = messages[messageIndex - 1];
                content = `Kullanıcı: ${userMessage.content}\n\nAI: ${message.content}`;
            } else {
                content = message.content;
            }
        } else {
            // Kullanıcı mesajı - tüm sohbeti al
            content = messages.map(msg => {
                const role = msg.role === 'user' ? 'Kullanıcı' : 'AI';
                return `${role}: ${msg.content}`;
            }).join('\n\n');
        }

        // İçerik önizlemesini göster (daha uzun önizleme, scroll yapılabilir)
        const preview = document.getElementById('ragContentPreview');
        const contentLength = document.getElementById('ragContentLength');
        const previewNote = document.getElementById('ragPreviewNote');
        
        if (preview) {
            // Önizleme için 2000 karakter göster (scroll yapılabilir)
            const previewLength = 2000;
            const truncated = content.length > previewLength 
                ? content.substring(0, previewLength) + '\n\n... (devamı kaydedilecek)' 
                : content;
            preview.textContent = truncated;
            
            // Karakter sayısını göster
            if (contentLength) {
                contentLength.textContent = `${content.length.toLocaleString('tr-TR')} karakter`;
            }
            
            // Not mesajını güncelle
            if (previewNote && content.length > previewLength) {
                previewNote.textContent = `Önizleme ilk ${previewLength.toLocaleString('tr-TR')} karakteri gösteriyor. Tam içerik (${content.length.toLocaleString('tr-TR')} karakter) kaydedilecektir.`;
            } else if (previewNote) {
                previewNote.textContent = 'Tam içerik kaydedilecektir.';
            }
        }

        // Başlık önerisi
        const titleInput = document.getElementById('ragDocumentTitle');
        if (titleInput && !titleInput.value) {
            const suggestedTitle = message.content.substring(0, 50).replace(/\n/g, ' ');
            titleInput.value = suggestedTitle + (message.content.length > 50 ? '...' : '');
        }

        // Kategorileri yükle
        await loadRAGCategories();

        // Modal'ı göster
        const modal = document.getElementById('ragLibraryModal');
        if (modal) {
            modal.classList.remove('hidden');
            lucide.createIcons(); // İkonları yeniden oluştur
        }
    }

    // Modal'ı kapat
    function closeRAGLibraryModal() {
        const modal = document.getElementById('ragLibraryModal');
        if (modal) {
            modal.classList.add('hidden');
        }
        currentRAGMessageId = null;
        // Formu temizle
        document.getElementById('ragDocumentTitle').value = '';
        document.getElementById('ragCategorySelect').value = '';
        document.getElementById('ragTags').value = '';
        document.getElementById('ragSummary').value = '';
        hideNewCategoryForm();
    }

    // Kategorileri yükle
    async function loadRAGCategories() {
        try {
            const response = await $.ajax({
                url: 'https://www.hepbilen.com/Multipurposectr/get_rag_categories',
                type: 'POST',
                dataType: 'json'
            });

            if (response.success) {
                ragCategories = response.categories || [];
                const select = document.getElementById('ragCategorySelect');
                if (select) {
                    // İlk seçeneği koru, diğerlerini temizle
                    select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Kategori seçin...</option>';
                    
                    ragCategories.forEach(category => {
                        const option = document.createElement('option');
                        option.value = category.id;
                        option.textContent = `${category.name} (${category.document_count || 0})`;
                        option.style.color = category.color || '#3b82f6';
                        select.appendChild(option);
                    });
                }
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Kategoriler yüklenirken hata:', error);
        }
    }

    // Yeni kategori formunu göster
    function showNewCategoryForm() {
        const form = document.getElementById('newCategoryForm');
        if (form) {
            form.classList.remove('hidden');
        }
    }

    // Yeni kategori formunu gizle
    function hideNewCategoryForm() {
        const form = document.getElementById('newCategoryForm');
        if (form) {
            form.classList.add('hidden');
            // Formu temizle
            document.getElementById('newCategoryName').value = '';
            document.getElementById('newCategoryDescription').value = '';
            document.getElementById('newCategoryColor').value = '#3b82f6';
            selectedCategoryColor = '#3b82f6';
        }
    }

    // Kategori rengi seç
    function selectCategoryColor(color) {
        selectedCategoryColor = color;
        document.getElementById('newCategoryColor').value = color;
        
        // Tüm renk butonlarının border'ını sıfırla
        document.querySelectorAll('[data-color]').forEach(btn => {
            btn.classList.remove('border-slate-600', 'ring-2', 'ring-offset-2');
            btn.classList.add('border-transparent');
        });
        
        // Seçilen rengin border'ını güncelle
        const selectedBtn = document.querySelector(`[data-color="${color}"]`);
        if (selectedBtn) {
            selectedBtn.classList.remove('border-transparent');
            selectedBtn.classList.add('border-slate-600', 'ring-2', 'ring-offset-2');
        }
    }

    // Yeni kategori oluştur
    async function createNewCategory() {
        const name = document.getElementById('newCategoryName').value.trim();
        const description = document.getElementById('newCategoryDescription').value.trim();
        const color = document.getElementById('newCategoryColor').value;

        if (!name) {
            alert('Kategori adı gereklidir');
            return;
        }

        try {
            const response = await $.ajax({
                url: 'https://www.hepbilen.com/Multipurposectr/create_rag_category',
                type: 'POST',
                data: {
                    name: name,
                    description: description,
                    color: color
                },
                dataType: 'json'
            });

            if (response.success) {
                // Kategorileri yeniden yükle
                await loadRAGCategories();
                
                // Yeni kategoriyi seç
                const select = document.getElementById('ragCategorySelect');
                if (select && response.category_id) {
                    select.value = response.category_id;
                }
                
                // Formu gizle
                hideNewCategoryForm();
            } else {
                alert(response.message || 'Kategori oluşturulurken bir hata oluştu');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Kategori oluşturma hatası:', error);
            alert('Kategori oluşturulurken bir hata oluştu');
        }
    }

    // RAG kütüphanesine kaydet
    async function saveToRAGLibrary() {
        const title = document.getElementById('ragDocumentTitle').value.trim();
        const categoryId = document.getElementById('ragCategorySelect').value;
        const tags = document.getElementById('ragTags').value.trim();
        const summary = document.getElementById('ragSummary').value.trim();

        // Validasyon
        if (!title) {
            alert('Başlık gereklidir');
            return;
        }

        if (!categoryId) {
            alert('Kategori seçmelisiniz');
            return;
        }

        if (!currentRAGMessageId) {
            alert('Mesaj bulunamadı');
            return;
        }

        const message = messages.find(msg => msg.id === currentRAGMessageId);
        if (!message) {
            alert('Mesaj bulunamadı');
            return;
        }

        // İçeriği hazırla
        let content = '';
        let sourceMessageIds = [currentRAGMessageId];
        
        if (message.role === 'assistant') {
            const messageIndex = messages.findIndex(msg => msg.id === currentRAGMessageId);
            if (messageIndex > 0) {
                const userMessage = messages[messageIndex - 1];
                content = `Kullanıcı: ${userMessage.content}\n\nAI: ${message.content}`;
                sourceMessageIds.push(userMessage.id);
            } else {
                content = message.content;
            }
        } else {
            // Tüm sohbeti kaydet
            content = messages.map(msg => {
                const role = msg.role === 'user' ? 'Kullanıcı' : 'AI';
                return `${role}: ${msg.content}`;
            }).join('\n\n');
            sourceMessageIds = messages.map(msg => msg.id);
        }

        // Etiketleri parse et
        const tagsArray = tags ? tags.split(',').map(t => t.trim()).filter(t => t) : [];

        // Kaydet butonunu devre dışı bırak
        const saveBtn = document.getElementById('ragSaveBtn');
        if (saveBtn) {
            saveBtn.disabled = true;
            saveBtn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="loader-2" class="w-4 h-4 animate-spin"></i> <span>Kaydediliyor...</span>';
            lucide.createIcons();
        }

        try {
            const response = await $.ajax({
                url: 'https://www.hepbilen.com/Multipurposectr/save_to_rag_library',
                type: 'POST',
                data: {
                    title: title,
                    category_id: categoryId,
                    content: content,
                    tags: JSON.stringify(tagsArray),
                    summary: summary,
                    source_chat_id: currentChatId || null,
                    source_message_ids: JSON.stringify(sourceMessageIds),
                    content_type: message.role === 'assistant' ? 'message' : 'conversation'
                },
                dataType: 'json'
            });

            if (response.success) {
                // Başarı mesajı
                alert('Sohbet başarıyla RAG kütüphanesine kaydedildi!');
                
                // Modal'ı kapat
                closeRAGLibraryModal();
            } else {
                alert(response.message || 'Kaydetme sırasında bir hata oluştu');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('RAG kaydetme hatası:', error);
            const errorMessage = error.responseJSON?.message || error.message || 'Bilinmeyen bir hata oluştu';
            alert('Kaydetme sırasında bir hata oluştu: ' + errorMessage);
            
            // Detaylı hata loglama
            if (error.responseJSON) {
                console.error('Backend Error Response:', error.responseJSON);
            }
            if (error.status) {
                console.error('HTTP Status:', error.status);
            }
        } finally {
            // Butonu tekrar aktif et
            if (saveBtn) {
                saveBtn.disabled = false;
                saveBtn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="save" class="w-4 h-4"></i> <span>Kütüphaneye Kaydet</span>';
                lucide.createIcons();
            }
        }
    }

    // Modal dışına tıklandığında kapat
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const modal = document.getElementById('ragLibraryModal');
        if (modal) {
            modal.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (e.target === modal) {
                    closeRAGLibraryModal();
                }
            });
        }
        
        const filtersModal = document.getElementById('ragFiltersModal');
        if (filtersModal) {
            filtersModal.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (e.target === filtersModal) {
                    closeRAGFiltersModal();
                }
            });
        }
    });

    // RAG Filtreleri
    let ragFilters = {
        minScore: null,
        categoryId: null,
        tags: [],
        dateFrom: null,
        dateTo: null,
        minUsageCount: null,
        sortBy: 'relevance' // relevance, date, usage, title
    };

    function openRAGFiltersModal() {
        const modal = document.getElementById('ragFiltersModal');
        if (modal) {
            modal.classList.remove('hidden');
            initializeIcons();
        }
    }

    function closeRAGFiltersModal() {
        const modal = document.getElementById('ragFiltersModal');
        if (modal) {
            modal.classList.add('hidden');
        }
    }

    function applyRAGFilters() {
        // Filtreleri topla
        ragFilters.minScore = document.getElementById('ragFilterMinScore')?.value || null;
        ragFilters.categoryId = document.getElementById('ragFilterCategory')?.value || null;
        ragFilters.sortBy = document.getElementById('ragFilterSortBy')?.value || 'relevance';
        
        // Tarih filtreleri
        const dateFrom = document.getElementById('ragFilterDateFrom')?.value;
        const dateTo = document.getElementById('ragFilterDateTo')?.value;
        ragFilters.dateFrom = dateFrom || null;
        ragFilters.dateTo = dateTo || null;
        
        closeRAGFiltersModal();
        
        // Filtre durumunu göster
        updateRAGFilterIndicator();
    }

    function clearRAGFilters() {
        ragFilters = {
            minScore: null,
            categoryId: null,
            tags: [],
            dateFrom: null,
            dateTo: null,
            minUsageCount: null,
            sortBy: 'relevance'
        };
        
        // Form'u temizle
        if (document.getElementById('ragFilterMinScore')) document.getElementById('ragFilterMinScore').value = '';
        if (document.getElementById('ragFilterCategory')) document.getElementById('ragFilterCategory').value = '';
        if (document.getElementById('ragFilterSortBy')) document.getElementById('ragFilterSortBy').value = 'relevance';
        if (document.getElementById('ragFilterDateFrom')) document.getElementById('ragFilterDateFrom').value = '';
        if (document.getElementById('ragFilterDateTo')) document.getElementById('ragFilterDateTo').value = '';
        
        updateRAGFilterIndicator();
    }

    function updateRAGFilterIndicator() {
        const hasFilters = ragFilters.minScore || ragFilters.categoryId || ragFilters.dateFrom || ragFilters.dateTo;
        const indicator = document.getElementById('ragFilterIndicator');
        if (indicator) {
            if (hasFilters) {
                indicator.classList.remove('hidden');
            } else {
                indicator.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        }
    }
</script>

<!-- RAG Filtreleri Modal -->
<div id="ragFiltersModal" class="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 z-50 hidden flex items-center justify-center p-4">
    <div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl max-w-lg w-full max-h-[90vh] overflow-hidden flex flex-col">
        <div class="px-6 py-4 border-b border-slate-200 flex items-center justify-between">
            <h3 class="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2">
                <i data-lucide="filter" class="w-5 h-5 text-emerald-600"></i>
                RAG Gelişmiş Filtreler
            </h3>
            <button onclick="closeRAGFiltersModal()" class="p-1.5 hover:bg-slate-100 rounded-full transition-colors">
                <i data-lucide="x" class="w-5 h-5 text-slate-500"></i>
            </button>
        </div>
        <div class="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
            <!-- Minimum Benzerlik Skoru -->
            <div>
                <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-2">Minimum Benzerlik Skoru (%)</label>
                <select id="ragFilterMinScore" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-300 rounded-lg text-sm focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:border-emerald-500">
                    <option value="">Tümü</option>
                    <option value="30">%30 ve üzeri</option>
                    <option value="50">%50 ve üzeri</option>
                    <option value="70">%70 ve üzeri</option>
                    <option value="90">%90 ve üzeri</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            
            <!-- Kategori -->
            <div>
                <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-2">Kategori</label>
                <select id="ragFilterCategory" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-300 rounded-lg text-sm focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:border-emerald-500">
                    <option value="">Tüm Kategoriler</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            
            <!-- Sıralama -->
            <div>
                <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-2">Sıralama</label>
                <select id="ragFilterSortBy" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-300 rounded-lg text-sm focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:border-emerald-500">
                    <option value="relevance">Benzerlik (Yüksek → Düşük)</option>
                    <option value="date">Tarih (Yeni → Eski)</option>
                    <option value="usage">Kullanım (Çok → Az)</option>
                    <option value="title">Başlık (A → Z)</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            
            <!-- Tarih Aralığı -->
            <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                <div>
                    <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-2">Başlangıç Tarihi</label>
                    <input type="date" id="ragFilterDateFrom" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-300 rounded-lg text-sm focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:border-emerald-500">
                </div>
                <div>
                    <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-2">Bitiş Tarihi</label>
                    <input type="date" id="ragFilterDateTo" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-300 rounded-lg text-sm focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-500 focus:border-emerald-500">
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="px-6 py-4 border-t border-slate-200 flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
            <button onclick="clearRAGFilters()" class="px-4 py-2 text-sm text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-800 hover:bg-slate-100 rounded-lg transition-colors">
                Temizle
            </button>
            <div class="flex gap-3">
                <button onclick="closeRAGFiltersModal()" class="px-4 py-2 text-sm text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-800 hover:bg-slate-100 rounded-lg transition-colors">
                    İptal
                </button>
                <button onclick="applyRAGFilters()" class="px-4 py-2 text-sm bg-emerald-600 text-white hover:bg-emerald-700 rounded-lg transition-colors">
                    Filtreleri Uygula
                </button>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<!-- RAG Filtre Göstergesi -->
<div id="ragFilterIndicator" class="fixed top-20 right-4 bg-emerald-50 border border-emerald-200 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 shadow-lg z-40 hidden">
    <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
        <i data-lucide="filter" class="w-4 h-4 text-emerald-600"></i>
        <span class="text-xs font-medium text-emerald-700">Filtreler Aktif</span>
        <button onclick="clearRAGFilters()" class="ml-2 text-emerald-600 hover:text-emerald-800">
            <i data-lucide="x" class="w-3 h-3"></i>
        </button>
    </div>
</div>

</script>
